
So GT = **(-0.2139)*T*epsilon + 82.10*epsilon + 94.205*epsilon^0.4475*exp(-6.616/T) + 5.1243*epsilon*exp(-(T-367.02)^2)**

The GT has these structural components:
1. **T*epsilon** (linear in both T and epsilon)
2. **epsilon** (linear in epsilon)
3. **epsilon^0.4475 * exp(-k/T)** (fractional power of epsilon times Arrhenius-type T dependence)

The key distinguishing features are:
- Term with **exp(-(T-c)^2)**: a Gaussian in T
- Term with **exp(-c/T)**: Arrhenius in T
